Text File : tokuseiinfo_syn
~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
When the Pokémon deals damage with its moves, there is a\n10% chance that targets will flinch.
Summons rain for 5 turns when the Pokémon enters a battle.
Boosts the Pokémon’s Speed stat by 1 stage at the end of\nevery turn.
Attacks landed on the Pokémon will never be critical hits.
If the Pokémon has full HP and takes damage from a move that\nwould knock it out in one hit, it will endure the hit with 1 HP.\nThe Pokémon is also immune to one-hit KO moves.
All Pokémon become unable to use explosive moves.\nExplosive Abilities also fail to trigger.
The Pokémon cannot be paralyzed.
Boosts the Pokémon’s evasiveness by 25% in a sandstorm.
When the Pokémon is hit by a contact move, the attacker has a\n30% chance of being paralyzed.
Electric-type moves do not work on the Pokémon. Instead, they\nrestore 1/4 of its max HP.
Water-type moves do not work on the Pokémon. Instead, they\nrestore 1/4 of its max HP.
The Pokémon cannot gain the Infatuated or Taunted statuses\nand is unaffected by Intimidate.
Eliminates the effects of weather.
Boosts the accuracy of the Pokémon’s moves by 30%.
The Pokémon cannot become drowsy or be put to sleep.
[~ 15]
The Pokémon cannot be poisoned or badly poisoned.
Fire-type moves do not work on the Pokémon. Instead, they\ngive the Pokémon the Flash Fire status.
The Pokémon is immune to additional effects from attacks.
The Pokémon cannot become confused and is unaffected by\nIntimidate.
The Pokémon is unaffected by the moves and held items of\nother Pokémon that would force it to switch out of battle.
When the Pokémon enters a battle, it lowers the Attack stats of\nopponents by 1 stage.
Opponents cannot be switched out of battle.
When the Pokémon is hit by a contact move, the attacker takes\ndamage equal to 1/8 of its max HP.
[~ 24]
The Pokémon floats off the ground, making it immune to\nGround-type moves, as well as the Spikes, Toxic Spikes,\nand Sticky Web statuses.
[~ 26]
If the Pokémon is burned, paralyzed, poisoned, or badly\npoisoned by another Pokémon’s move or Ability, that Pokémon\nwill also be inflicted with the same status condition.
The Pokémon’s stats cannot be lowered by other Pokémon’s\nmoves or Abilities.
The Pokémon’s status conditions are cured when it switches out\nof battle.
The Pokémon draws in all Electric-type moves. These moves do\nnot work on the Pokémon. Instead, they boost its Sp. Atk stat by\n1 stage.
[~ 31]
Doubles the Pokémon’s Speed stat in rain.
Doubles the Pokémon’s Speed stat in harsh sunlight.
The Pokémon ignores changes to targets’ evasiveness and its\naccuracy cannot be lowered.
When the Pokémon enters a battle, it changes its Ability to\nmatch that of an opponent.
Doubles the power of the Pokémon’s physical moves.
When the Pokémon is hit by a contact move, the attacker has a\n30% chance of being poisoned.
The Pokémon never flinches when attacked and is unaffected\nby Intimidate.
The Pokémon cannot be frozen.
[~ 40]
[~ 41]
The Pokémon is immune to sound-based moves.
The Pokémon has 1/16 of its max HP restored at the end of\nevery turn in rain.
Summons a sandstorm for 5 turns when the Pokémon enters\na battle.
Causes opponents to expend 1 more PP when using moves\nagainst the Pokémon.
Halves the damage the Pokémon takes from Fire- and Ice-type\nmoves.
The Pokémon awakens from sleep twice as fast as other\nPokémon.
When the Pokémon is hit by a contact move, the attacker has a\n30% chance of being burned.
[~ 49]
The Pokémon ignores changes to targets’ evasiveness and its\naccuracy cannot be lowered.
The Pokémon’s Attack stat cannot be lowered by other\nPokémon’s moves or Abilities.
If the Pokémon is not already holding an item, at the end of\nthe turn it will pick up an item that was consumed by another\nPokémon.
[~ 53]
When the Pokémon uses physical moves, its Attack stat is\nboosted by 50%, but its accuracy is lowered by 20%.
When the Pokémon is hit by a contact move, the attacker has\na 30% chance of gaining the Infatuated status if the attacker\nand the Pokémon are of opposite genders.
Boosts the Pokémon’s Sp. Atk stat by 50% if an ally with the\nPlus or Minus Ability is also in battle.
Boosts the Pokémon’s Sp. Atk stat by 50% if an ally with the\nPlus or Minus Ability is also in battle.
The Pokémon transforms with the weather to change its type to\nWater, Fire, or Ice.
The Pokémon’s held item cannot be stolen or removed by other\nPokémon.
The Pokémon has a 30% chance of curing its own status\nconditions at the end of every turn.
When the Pokémon has a status condition, its Attack stat is\nboosted by 50%. Being burned does not halve the damage\ndealt by the Pokémon’s physical moves.
When the Pokémon has a status condition, its Defense stat is\nboosted by 50%.
[~ 63]
Boosts the power of the Pokémon’s Grass-type moves by 50%\nwhen its HP drops to 1/3 or less of its max.
Boosts the power of the Pokémon’s Fire-type moves by 50%\nwhen its HP drops to 1/3 or less of its max.
